  <script data-pagespeed-no-defer="" pagespeed_no_defer="">
   (function() {
            function getExperimentStates(filter) {
                return window.optimizely.get('state').getExperimentStates(filter);
            }

            function isExperimentActive(id) {
                return Object.keys(getExperimentStates({ isActive: true })).includes(id);
            }

            function waitForConsent(cb) {
                if (!window.__tcfapi) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        waitForConsent(cb);
                    }, 50);
                    return;
                }

                var callback = function (tcData, success) {
                    if (success && (tcData.eventStatus === 'tcloaded' || tcData.eventStatus === 'useractioncomplete')) {
                        window.__tcfapi("checkConsent", 2, function (consent, success) {
                            success && consent && cb && cb();
                        }, {
                            data: [{
                                vendorId: 10083
                            }]
                        });
                    }
                };

                window.__tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, callback);            
            }

            // Array of the experiments' state by experiment id
            var experimentsPromises = {};
            var experimentIds = new Set();

            function getExperimentObj(experimentId) {
                experimentIds.add(experimentId);
                var currentExperimentPromise = experimentsPromises[experimentId];
                if (currentExperimentPromise == null) {
                    var outsideResolve, outsideReject;
                    var experimentPromise = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                        outsideResolve = resolve;
                    });
                    var experimentPromiseObj = {
                        _resolve: outsideResolve,
                        promise: experimentPromise
                    };
                    experimentsPromises[experimentId] = experimentPromiseObj;
                    return experimentPromiseObj;
                } else {
                    return currentExperimentPromise;
                }
            }

            var experiments = {
                get: function(experimentId) {
                    window.optimizelyReady.then(function(_) {
                        var experimentState = getExperimentStates()[experimentId];
                        if (experimentState && !experimentState.isActive) {
                            getExperimentObj(experimentId)._resolve({ error: 'The experiment is not active' });
                        } else if (!experimentState) {
                            getExperimentObj(experimentId)._resolve({
                                error: 'Experiment id not found: check if correct'
                            });
                        }
                    });
                    return getExperimentObj(experimentId).promise;
                }
            };

            window.optimizely = window.optimizely || [];

            window.optimizely.push({
                type: 'addListener',
                filter: {
                    type: 'lifecycle',
                    name: 'campaignDecided'
                },
                handler: function(event) {
                    var id = event.data.decision.experimentId;
                    var experimentObj = getExperimentObj(id);
                    var experimentData = getExperimentStates()[id];
                    if (experimentData && experimentData.isActive) {
                        if (experimentData.isInExperimentHoldback) {
                            experimentObj._resolve({ error: 'The experiment is in holdback' });
                        } else {
                            experimentObj._resolve(event.data);
                        }
                    } else {
                        experimentObj._resolve({ error: 'The experiment is not active' });
                    }
                }
            });
            window.optimizelyHelper = {
                get: experiments.get.bind(experiments)
            };
            window.optimizelyReady = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                window.optimizely.push({
                    type: 'addListener',
                    filter: {
                        type: 'lifecycle',
                        name: 'initialized'
                    },
                    handler: function() {
                        var state = window.optimizely.get('state');
                        resolve({ optimizely: window.optimizely, state: state, variationMap: state.getVariationMap() });
                    }
                });

                waitForConsent(function() {
                    var script = document.createElement('script');
                    var ref = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
                    script.onerror = reject;
                    script.src = 'https://cdn.optimizely.com/js/17853600003.js';
                    ref.parentNode.insertBefore(script, ref);
                });
            });

            var as24optimizely = Object.assign(Object.create(HTMLElement.prototype), {
                attachedCallback: function() {
                    window.optimizely = window.optimizely || [];
                    var action = this.getAttribute('action');
                    if (action == 'push') {
                        var payload = JSON.parse(this.getAttribute('payload'));
                        window.optimizely.push(payload);
                    }
                }
            });
            document.registerElement('as24-optimizely', { prototype: as24optimizely });
        })();
  </script>

      <script type="application/javascript">
       document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', toggleShowSlices);

        function toggleShowSlices(){
            var vehicleDataString = window.localStorage.getItem('vehicleData');
            if (vehicleDataString){
                var vehicleData = JSON.parse(vehicleDataString);
                if (validate(vehicleData)) {
                    var personalizedElm = document.getElementById('personalized');

                    personalizedElm.getElementsByClassName('vehicleData-make')[0].textContent = vehicleData.make;
                    personalizedElm.getElementsByClassName('vehicleData-date')[0].textContent = new Date(vehicleData.dateCreated).toLocaleDateString('de-DE', {
                        day: '2-digit',
                        month: '2-digit',
                        year: 'numeric'
                    });
                    personalizedElm.getElementsByClassName('vehicleData')[0].textContent = vehicleData.make + " " + vehicleData.model + " (" + Number(vehicleData.mileage).toLocaleString("de-DE") + " km, " + vehicleData.transmission + ", " + vehicleData.power + " kW)";
                    personalizedElm.style.display = "block";
                    return;
                }
            }

            var nonPersonalizedElm = document.getElementById("nonPersonalized");
            nonPersonalizedElm.style.display = "block";

            function validate(vehicleData){
                return vehicleData.make &&
                        vehicleData.model &&
                        vehicleData.transmission &&
                        vehicleData.mileage &&
                        vehicleData.power &&
                        vehicleData.dateCreated
            }
        }
      </script>

    <section class="as24-section as24-link-columns">
     <div class="as24-link-columns__header">
      <h1 class="sc-font-xl sc-text-center">
       Gebrauchtwagen gesucht?
       <span class="sc-font-l sc-block-center">
        Entdecke hier das Angebot von AutoScout24
       </span>
      </h1>
     </div>
     <div class="as24-link-columns__row">
      <div class="as24-link-columns__column sc-expandable-box sc-expandable-box--adaptive">
       <input class="sc-expandable-box__toggle" id="list1-1" type="checkbox"/>
       <h4 class="as24-link-columns__label sc-expandable-box__title">
        <label class="sc-expandable-box__label" for="list1-1">
         audi
        </label>
       </h4>

    <div class="opt-wysiwyg">
     <h2 class="sc-font-xl sc-text-center" id="opt-wysiwyg-headline">
      Lass deinen Autotraum wahr werden mit AutoScout24, dem europaweit größten Online-Automarkt!
     </h2>
     <p>
      Weit mehr als zwei Millionen Fahrzeuge, von denen jedes deins sein könnte, aus dem Angebot von über 50.000 Händlern und Verkäufern, die auf deine Anfrage warten: Das macht AutoScout24 zum europaweit größten Online-Automarkt. Rund um das Thema Fahrzeuge und Mobilität bleiben hier weder Fragen noch Wünsche offen.
     </p>
     <p>
      Fährst du öfter in die Berge und suchst einen Geländewagen oder SUV mit Allradantrieb? In unserem Marken- und Modellkatalog findest du alle Informationen sowie unzählige Angebote vom größten bis zum kleinsten Offroader. Oder bist du eher ein Stadtmensch und wünschst dir einen umweltfreundlichen und wendigen Kleinwagen etwa von Fiat, VW oder Mini? In unserem Fahrzeugmarkt findest du mit wenigen Klicks das Modell, das genau deinen Vorstellungen entspricht, und zwar mit Direktkontakt zum Verkäufer oder Händler.
     </p>
     <p>
      Vom einfachen Nutzfahrzeug bis zum Luxus-Sportwagen, vom Oldtimer bis zur modernen Oberklassenlimousine und vom Motorrad bis zu den Quads und Trikes – bei AutoScout24 stehst du vor einem überdimensionalen Parkhaus, das für jeden Fahrzeugsucher das Richtige bereit hält, und behältst dabei den vollen Überblick:
     </p>
     <p>
      Welche Eigenschaften deines zukünftigen Autos sind dir wichtig? Bestimme selbst, was du findest, indem du über die Fahrzeug-Schnellsuche die Marke, das Modell, die Kraftstoffart, den Kilometerstand und den Preis vorgibst. Wenn du möchtest, wähle auch gleich die Bauart, die Farbe, die Art der Ausstattung oder andere Daten, die dir wichtig sind. Falls du ein neues Auto, ein Fahrzeug mit Tageszulassung oder einen Jahreswagen suchst, stell dir dein Wunschmodell ganz individuell mit dem Neuwagen-Konfigurator zusammen.
     </p>
     <p>
      Doch das ist längst nicht alles: Über das AutoScout24-Magazin, die Ratgeber oder das Autolexikon erhältst du mitunter Zugang zu den besten Werkstätten, das optimale Tuning, das passende Zubehör, die richtige Finanzierung, die günstigste Kfz-Versicherung und vieles mehr.
     </p>
    </div>

        /** In case we don't have a visitor id we set one. */
        function ensureVisitorId() {
            if (!/as24Visitor/.test(document.cookie)) {
                var domain = window.location.hostname.replace('www.', '').replace('local.', '');
                document.cookie = 'as24Visitor=' + uuidv4() + ';path=/;max-age=31536000;domain=' + domain;
            }
        }

        /** Apps have their own CMP. For webviews they provide the consent string through query strings. */
        function setCmpCookiesIfProvidedAsQueryStrings() {
            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            var euconsentv2 = urlParams.get('euconsent-v2');
            var cconsentv2 = urlParams.get('cconsent-v2');
            var gdprAuditId = urlParams.get('gdpr-auditId');
            var addtlConsent = urlParams.get('addtl_consent');
            var gdprLastInteraction = (Date.now() / 1000).toFixed(3);

            var domain = 'domain=' + document.location.hostname.replace('www.', '').replace('local.', '');
            var path = 'path=/';
            var maxAge = 'max-age=31536000';
            var sameSite = 'samesite=Lax';

            if (euconsentv2 && cconsentv2 && gdprAuditId && addtlConsent) {
                document.cookie = ['euconsent-v2=' + euconsentv2, path, maxAge, domain, sameSite].join(';');
                document.cookie = ['cconsent-v2=' + cconsentv2, path, maxAge, domain, sameSite].join(';');
                document.cookie = ['gdpr-auditId=' + gdprAuditId, path, maxAge, domain, sameSite].join(';');
                document.cookie = ['addtl_consent=' + addtlConsent, path, maxAge, domain, sameSite].join(';');
                document.cookie = ['gdpr-last-interaction=' + gdprLastInteraction, path, maxAge, domain, sameSite].join(
                    ';'
                );
            }
        }

        /**
            We take the language from the domain and path and set it for the CMP.
            For non-core countries we always set it to 'en'.

            @param {string} tld - The top level domain
            @param {string} pathname - The full page path
         */
        function setCmpLanguage(tld, pathname) {
            function guessLanguage() {
                switch (tld) {
                    case 'at':
                        return 'de';
                    case 'be':
                        return pathname.indexOf('/fr/') === 0 ? 'fr' : 'nl';
                    case 'lu':
                        return 'fr';
                    case 'de':
                    case 'it':
                    case 'nl':
                    case 'fr':
                    case 'es':
                        return tld;
                    default:
                        return 'en';
                }
            }

            __tcfapi('changeLanguage', null, noOp, guessLanguage());
        }

        function trackCmpEvents() {
            function trackInGA(event) {
                window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

                if (
                    dataLayer.filter(function (x) {
                        return x.event === 'data_ready';
                    }).length === 0
                ) {
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        trackInGA(event);
                    }, 100);
                    return;
                }

                window.dataLayer.push({
                    event: 'event_trigger',
                    event_category: 'CMP',
                    event_action: event,
                });
            }
            var trackedCmpEvents = [
                'acceptAllButtonClicked',
                'exitButtonClicked',
                'saveAndExitButtonClicked',
                'consentToolShouldBeShown',
                'denyAllButtonClicked',
                'consentManagerDisplayed',
                'consentManagerClosed',
                'consentNoticeDisplayed',
                'consentNoticeClosed',
            ];

            trackedCmpEvents.forEach(function (event) {
                window.__tcfapi(
                    'addEventListener',
                    2,
                    function () {
                        trackInGA(event);
                    },
                    event
                );
            });
        }

        function loadLiveRampScript(uid) {
            var script = document.createElement('script');
            var ref = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
            ref.parentNode.insertBefore(script, ref);
            script.src = 'https://gdpr-wrapper.privacymanager.io/gdpr/' + uid + '/gdpr-liveramp.js';
        }

        function hideCmpIfNeeded() {
            var isOnPrivacyPage = document.querySelector('as24-tracking[pageid="au-company-privacy"]');
            var containsSuppressCmpAttribute = document.querySelector('body[data-suppress-cmp="true"]') !== null;
            
            var shouldHideCmp =
                window.location.hostname === 'accounts.autoscout24.com' || // on Identity pages
                isOnPrivacyPage || // on privacy pages
                containsSuppressCmpAttribute || // explicit suppress directive
                window.self !== window.top; // inside an iframe

            var suppressDialogue = function () {
                __tcfapi('toggleConsentTool', 2, function () {}, false);
            };

            if (shouldHideCmp) {
                __tcfapi('addEventListener', 2, suppressDialogue);

                if (isOnPrivacyPage || containsSuppressCmpAttribute) {
                    window.addEventListener('load', function () {
                        __tcfapi('removeEventListener', 2, suppressDialogue);
                    });
                }
            }
        }

        function noOp() {}

        function loadCmpWithoutAbTest() {
            var tldToLiveRampMap = {
                at: '3e24114e-f793-4eba-8c0f-735086de7eb6',
                be: '55b58bfe-4c4d-4943-bbf3-11ec3eedc57b',

            loadLiveRampScript(liverampTcf2Id);
        }

        function loadCmpWithAbTest() {
            var userId = getCookieValue('as24Visitor');

            fetchExperimentData(userId).then(function (data) {
                function sendEvent(event) {
                    var url =
                        'https://cmp-optimizely-fs.as24-media.eu-west-1.infinity.as24.tech/sendevent/' +
                        data.userid +
                        '/' +
                        event;

                    if ('sendBeacon' in navigator) {
                        navigator.sendBeacon(url);
                    } else {
                        new Image().src = url;
                    }
                }

                function trackEventInOptimizely(cmpEvent, optimizelyEvent) {
                    window.__tcfapi(
                        'addEventListener',
                        2,
                        () => {
                            sendEvent(optimizelyEvent);
                        },
                        cmpEvent
                    );
                }

                trackEventInOptimizely('acceptAllButtonClicked', 'cmpAcceptAll');
                trackEventInOptimizely('saveAndExitButtonClicked', 'cmpSaveAndExit');
                trackEventInOptimizely('exitButtonClicked', 'cmpExit');
                trackEventInOptimizely('saveAndExitButtonClicked', 'cmpExit');
                trackEventInOptimizely('acceptAllButtonClicked', 'cmpExit');
                trackEventInOptimizely('consentToolShouldBeShown', 'cmpShown');
                trackEventInOptimizely('consentNoticeDisplayed', 'cmpNoticeDisplayed');

                if (window.location.pathname.startsWith('/angebote/')) {
                    window.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                        if (!e || !e.target || !e.target.closest) {
                            return;
                        }

                        var isCallButton = !!e.target.closest('a[href^="tel:"]');
                        if (isCallButton) {
                            sendEvent('cmpCall');
                            return;
                        }

                        var isEmailButton = !!e.target.closest('[data-cip-id="submit"]');
                        if (isEmailButton) {
                            sendEvent('cmpEmail');
                            return;
                        }
                    });
                }

                var liverampIdByVariation = {
                    variation_1: '7fa21d14-bb68-4b5e-b85f-b5ae26b92696', // original IT
                    variation_2: '0ea30077-436d-4294-a85e-0af92282c3ea',
                    variation_3: 'b36f31e9-ba65-47f5-b151-66c307c999d9',
                    variation_4: '00527a4c-e2b6-4933-a80f-4e8792b153d4',
                };

                var liverampid = liverampIdByVariation[data.variation];

                loadLiveRampScript(liverampid);
            });
        }

        /**
            Reads cookie value
            @param {string} cookieName
            @return {string}
        */
        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            var x = document.cookie.match('(^|;)\\s*' + cookieName + '\\s*=\\s*([^;]+)');
            return x ? x.pop() : '';
        }

        /** Generates a UUID v4
            @return {string}
        */
        function uuidv4() {
            return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function (c) {
                var r = (Math.random() * 16) | 0,
                    v = c == 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3) | 0x8;
                return v.toString(16);
            });
        }

        /**
            @param {string} userId
            @return {Promise<{ data: { userid: string; variation: string; } }>}
        */
        function fetchExperimentData(userId) {
            var optimizelyUrl = 'https://cmp-optimizely-fs.as24-media.eu-west-1.infinity.as24.tech/activate/';
            var experimentUrl = optimizelyUrl + 'cmp_theme_comparison_it/';

            return fetch(experimentUrl + userId).then(function (r) {
                return r.json();
            });
        }
    })();
